Baptism of Fire" (1940), also known as "Feuertaufe", is a powerful documentary film that captures the early days of World War II. As Poland becomes the first victim of Hitler's blitzkrieg, the movie provides a harrowing portrayal of German aerial campaigns, showing the meticulous preparations for flight, the sheer brutality of air strikes, and the heart-wrenching destruction of Poland's towns and armies. The original score by Norbert Schultze adds a poignant, lyrical touch to this chilling Nazi propaganda film, further highlighting the dark themes of war and propaganda.
